166→\t\t\tif ids[panelID] {\n   167→\t\t\t\t// Duplicate ID found, assign new one\n   168→\t\t\t\tpanel[\"id\"] = float64(nextPanelId)\n   169→\t\t\t\tnextPanelId++\n   170→\t\t\t} else {\n   171→\t\t\t\t// Valid unique ID, keep it\n   172→\t\t\t\tids[panelID] = true\n   173→\t\t\t}\n   174→\t\t} else {\n   175→\t\t\t// No ID or invalid ID, assign new one\n   176→\t\t\tpanel[\"id\"] = float64(nextPanelId)\n   177→\t\t\tnextPanelId++\n   178→\t\t}\n   179→\t}\n   180→}\n   181→\n   182→// getNextPanelId finds the next available panel ID\n   183→func getNextPanelId(panels []map[string]interface{}) int {\n   184→\tmax := 0\n   185→\tfor _, panel := range panels {\n   186→\t\tif panelID, ok := panel[\"id\"].(float64); ok && panelID > 0 {\n   187→\t\t\tif int(panelID) > max {\n   188→\t\t\t\tmax = int(panelID)\n   189→\t\t\t}\n   190→\t\t}\n   191→\t}\n   192→\treturn max + 1\n   193→}\n   194→\n   195→// sortPanelsByGridPos sorts panels by grid position (y first, then x)\n   196→func sortPanelsByGridPos(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   197→\tpanels := getPanels(dashboard)\n   198→\tif len(panels) == 0 {\n   199→\t\treturn\n   200→\t}\n   201→\n   202→\tsort.SliceStable(panels, func(i, j int) bool {\n   203→\t\tpanelA := panels[i]\n   204→\t\tpanelB := panels[j]\n   205→\n   206→\t\tgridPosA, okA := panelA[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   207→\t\tgridPosB, okB := panelB[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   208→\n   209→\t\tif !okA || !okB {\n   210→\t\t\treturn false\n   211→\t\t}\n   212→\n   213→\t\tyA, okA := gridPosA[\"y\"].(float64)\n   214→\t\tyB, okB := gridPosB[\"y\"].(float64)\n   215→\n   216→\t\tif !okA || !okB {\n   217→\t\t\treturn false\n   218→\t\t}\n   219→\n   220→\t\tif yA == yB {\n   221→\t\t\t// Same row, sort by x\n   222→\t\t\txA, okA := gridPosA[\"x\"].(float64)\n   223→\t\t\txB, okB := gridPosB[\"x\"].(float64)\n   224→\n   225→\t\t\tif !okA || !okB {\n   226→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   227→\t\t\t}\n   228→\n   229→\t\t\treturn xA < xB\n   230→\t\t}\n   231→\n   232→\t\treturn yA < yB\n   233→\t})\n   234→}\n   235→\n   236→// addBuiltInAnnotationQuery adds the built-in \"Annotations & Alerts\" annotation\n   237→func addBuiltInAnnotationQuery(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   238→\tannotations, ok := dashboard[\"annotations\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   239→\tif !ok {\n   240→\t\treturn\n   241→\t}\n   242→\n   243→\tlist, ok := annotations[\"list\"].([]interface{})\n   244→\tif !ok {\n {\n   251→\t\t\tif builtIn, ok := annotation[\"builtIn\"].(float64); ok && builtIn == 1 {\n   252→\t\t\t\treturn // Already exists\n   253→\t\t\t}\n   254→\t\t}\n   255→\t}\n   256→\n   257→\t// Add built-in annotation\n   258→\tbuiltInAnnotation := map[string]interface{}{\n   259→\t\t\"datasource\": map[string]interface{}{\n   260→\t\t\t\"uid\":  \"-- Grafana --\",\n   261→\t\t\t\"type\": \"grafana\",\n   262→\t\t},\n   263→\t\t\"name\":      \"Annotations & Alerts\",\n   264→\t\t\"type\":      \"dashboard\",\n   265→\t\t\"iconColor\": \"rgba(0, 211, 255, 1)\", // 272→\tannotations[\"list\"] = append([]interface{}{builtInAnnotation}, list...)\n   273→}\n   274→\n   275→// initMeta initializes meta properties with defaults\n   276→func initMeta(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   277→\tmeta, ok := dashboard[\"meta\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   278→\tif !ok {\n   279→\t\tmeta = make(map[string]interface{})\n   280→\t\tdashboard[\"meta\"] = meta\n   281→\t}\n   282→\n   283→\t// Apply defaults\n   284→\tif meta[\"canShare\"] == nil {\n   285→\t\tmeta[\"canShare\"] = true\n   286→\t}\n   287→\tif meta[\"canSave\"] == nil {\n 301→\tmeta[\"showSettings\"] = meta[\"canEdit\"]\n   302→\n   303→\teditable, _ := dashboard[\"editable\"].(bool)\n   304→\tif meta[\"canSave\"] == true && !editable {\n 317→\t}\n   318→}\n   319→\n   320→// removeNullValuesFromVariables removes null values from variable.current.value\n   321→func removeNullValuesFromVariables(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   322→\ttemplating, ok := dashboard[\"templating\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   323→\tif !ok {\n   324→\t\treturn\n   325→\t}\n   326→\n   327→\tlist, ok := templating[\"list\"].([]interface{})\n   328→\tif !ok || len(list) == 0 {\n   329→\t\treturn\n   330→\t}\n   331→\n   332→\tfor _, item := range list {\n   333→\t\tif variable, ok := item.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   334→\t\t\tif value == nil {\n   338→\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(current, \"value\")\n   339→\t\t\t\t\t} else if valueArray, isArray := value.([]interface{}); isArray {\n   340→\t\t\t\t\t\t// Check for null values in arrays\n   341→\t\t\t\t\t\thasNull := false\n   342→\t\t\t\t\t\tfor _, v := range valueArray {\n   343→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif v == nil {\n   344→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\thasNull = true\n   345→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   346→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   347→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   348→\t\t\t\t\t\tif hasNull {\n   349→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(current, \"value\")\n   350→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   351→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   352→\t\t\t\t}\n   353→\t\t\t}\n   354→\t\t}\n   355→\t}\n   356→}\n   357→\n   358→// ensureQueryIds ensures all queries have refId\n   359→func ensureQueryIds(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n   360→\ttargets, ok := panel[\"targets\"].([]interface{})\n   361→\tif !ok || len(targets) == 0 {\n   362→\t\treturn\n   363→\t}\n   364→\n   365→\t// Check if any target is missing refId\n   366→\thasMissingRefId := false\n   367→\tfor _, target := range targets {\n   368→\t\tif targetMap, ok := target.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   369→\t\t\tif targetMap[\"refId\"] == nil {\n   370→\t\t\t\thasMissingRefId = true\n   371→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   372→\t\t\t}\n   373→\t\t}\n   374→\t}\n   375→\n   376→\tif hasMissingRefId {\n   377→\t\t// Find existing refIds\n   378→\t\texistingRefIds := make(map[string]bool)\n   379→\t\tfor _, target := range targets {\n   380→\t\t\tif targetMap, ok := target.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   381→\t\t\t\tif refId, ok := targetMap[\"refId\"].(string); ok {\n   382→\t\t\t\t\texistingRefIds[refId] = true\n   383→\t\t\t\t}\n   384→\t\t\t}\n   385→\t\t}\n   386→\n   387→\t\t// Assign refIds to targets that don't have them\n   388→\t\tletters := \"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ\"\n   389→\t\tletterIndex := 0\n   390→\n   391→\t\tfor _, target := range targets {\n   392→\t\t\tif targetMap, ok := target.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   393→\t\t\t\tif targetMap[\"refId\"] == nil {\n   394→\t\t\t\t\t// Find next available refId\n   395→\t\t\t\t\tfor letterIndex < len(letters) {\n   396→\t\t\t\t\t\trefId := string(letters[letterIndex])\n   397→\t\t\t\t\t\tif !existingRefIds[refId] {\n   398→\t\t\t\t\t\t\ttargetMap[\"refId\"] = refId\n   399→\t\t\t\t\t\t\texistingRefIds[refId] = true\n   400→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   401→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   402→\t\t\t\t\t\tletterIndex++\n   403→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   404→\t\t\t\t\tletterIndex++\n   405→\t\t\t\t}\n   406→\t\t\t}\n   407→\t\t}\n   408→\t}\n   409→}\n   410→\n   411→// getPanels extracts all panels from the dashboard (including nested panels)\n   412→// This matches the frontend's depth-first iteration order in panelIterator()\n   413→func getPanels(dashboard map[string]interface{}) []map[string]interface{} {\n   414→\tvar panels []map[string]interface{}\n   415→\n   416→\t// Get top-level panels\n   417→\tif dashboardPanels, 420→\t\t\t\t// Add top-level panel first\n   421→\t\t\t\tpanels = append(panels, panel)\n   422→\n   423→\t\t\t\t// Then add its nested panels (depth-first order)\n   424→\t\t\t\tif nestedPanels, ok := panel[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n   425→\t\t\t\t\tfor _, nestedPanelInterface := range nestedPanels {\n   426→\t\t\t\t\t\tif nestedPanel, ok := nestedPanelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   427→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tpanels = append(panels, nestedPanel)\n   428→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   429→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   430→\t\t\t\t}\n   431→\t\t\t}\n   432→\t\t}\n   433→\t}\n   434→\n   435→\treturn panels\n   436→}\n   437→\n   438→// cleanupPanelForSaveWithContext mimics the PanelModel.getSaveModel() behavior\n   439→// This removes properties that shouldn't be persisted and filters out default values\n   440→func cleanupPanelForSaveWithContext(panel map[string]interface{}, isNested bool) {\n   441→\t// Apply auto-migration logic (matches frontend PanelModel constructor)\n   442→\t// This happens during cleanup phase to match when frontend applies auto-migration\n   443→\t// Only apply auto-migration to top-level panels, not nested ones (matches frontend behavior)\n   444→\tif !isNested {\n   445→\t\tapplyPanelAutoMigration(panel)\n   446→\t}\n   447→\n   448→\t// Library panel specific cleanup (matches frontend behavior)\n   449→\t// Frontend only preserves id, title, gridPos, and libraryPanel for library panels\n   450→\tif libraryPanel, hasLibraryPanel := panel[\"libraryPanel\"]; hasLibraryPanel && libraryPanel != nil {\n   451→\t\t// Create a new panel with only the essential properties\n   452→\t\tessentialProps := map[string]interface{}{\n   453→\t\t\t\"id\":           panel[\"id\"],\n   454→\t\t\t\"title\":        panel[\"title\"],\n   455→\t\t\t\"gridPos\":      panel[\"gridPos\"],\n   456→\t\t\t\"libraryPanel\": libraryPanel,\n   457→\t\t}\n   458→\n   459→\t\t// Clear the original panel and copy back only essential properties\n   460→\t\tfor key := range panel {\n   461→\t\t\tdelete(panel, key)\n   462→\t\t}\n   463→\t\tfor key, value := range essentialProps {\n   464→\t\t\tif value != nil {\n   465→\t\t\t\tpanel[key] = value\n   466→\t\t\t}\n   467→\t\t}\n   468→\t\treturn // Skip the rest of the cleanup for library panels\n   469→\t}\n   470→\n   471→\t// Row panel specific cleanup (matches frontend behavior)\n   472→\tcleanupRowPanelProperties(panel)\n   473→\n   474→\t// Track which properties were present in the input to preserve them even if they become empty\n   475→\toriginalProperties := make(map[string]bool)\n   476→\tfor key := range panel {\n   477→\t\toriginalProperties[key] = true\n   478→\t}\n   479→\t// Properties that should never be persisted (notPersistedProperties)\n   480→\tnotPersistedProps := map[string]bool{\n   481→\t\t\"events\":                  true,\n   482→\t\t\"isViewing\":               true,\n   483→\t\t\"isEditing\":               true,\n   484→\t\t\"isInView\":                true,\n   485→\t\t\"hasRefreshed\":            true,\n   486→\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\":     true, // This is the key one causing issues\n   487→\t\t\"plugin\":                  true,\n   488→\t\t\"queryRunner\":             true,\n   489→\t\t\"replaceVariables\":        true,\n   490→\t\t\"configRev\":               true,\n   491→\t\t\"hasSavedPanelEditChange\": true,\n   492→\t\t\"getDisplayTitle\":         true,\n   493→\t\t\"dataSupport\":             true,\n   494→\t\t\"key\":                     true,\n   495→\t\t\"isNew\":                   true,\n   496→\t\t\"refreshWhenInView\":       true,\n   497→\t\t\"scopedVars\":              true, // Frontend removes scopedVars from save model\n   498→\t}\n   499→\n   500→\t// Default values that should be filtered out if they match (defaults)\n   501→\tdefaults := map[string]interface{}{\n   502→\t\t\"gridPos\": map[string]interface{}{\n   503→\t\t\t\"x\": float64(0), \"y\": float64(0), \"h\": float64(3), \"w\": float64(6),\n   504→\t\t},\n   505→\t\t\"targets\": []interface{}{\n   506→\t\t\tmap[string]interface{}{\"refId\": \"A\"},\n   507→\t\t},\n   508→\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\": map[string]interface{}{},\n   509→\t\t\"transparent\":         false,\n   510→\t\t\"options\":             map[string]interface{}{},\n   511→\t\t\"links\":               []interface{}{},\n   512→\t\t\"fieldConfig\": map[string]interface{}{\n   513→\t\t\t\"defaults\":  map[string]interface{}{},\n   514→\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n   515→\t\t},\n   516→\t\t\"title\": \"\",\n   517→\t}\n   518→\n   519→\t// Remove notPersistedProperties\n   520→\tfor prop := range notPersistedProps {\n   521→\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   522→\t}\n   523→\n   524→\t// Filter out properties that match defaults\n   525→\tfor prop, defaultValue := range defaults {\n   526→\t\tif panelValue, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n   527→\t\t\tif isEqual(panelValue, defaultValue) {\n   528→\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   529→\t\t\t}\n   530→\t\t}\n   531→\t}\n   532→\n   533→\t// Remove empty transformations array unless nested panel had them originally\n   534→\tif transformations, ok := panel[\"transformations\"].([]interface{}); ok && len(transformations) == 0 {\n   535→\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadTransformations\"] != true || !isNested {\n   536→\t\t\tdelete(panel, \"transformations\")\n   537→\t\t}\n   538→\t}\n   539→\n   540→\t// Remove null values recursively to match frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior\n   541→\t// Pass panel type information to help with threshold handling\n   542→\tpanelType := \"\"\n   543→\tif t, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n   544→\t\tpanelType = t\n   545→\t}\n   546→\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(panel, panelType)\n   547→\n   548→\t// Filter out properties that match defaults (matches frontend's isEqual logic)\n   549→\tfilterDefaultValues(panel, originalProperties)\n   550→\n   551→\t// Clean up internal markers\n   552→\tdelete(panel, \"_originallyHadTransformations\")\n   553→\tdelete(panel, \"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\")\n   554→}\n   555→\n   556→// filterDefaultValues removes properties that match the default values (matches frontend's isEqual logic)\n   557→func filterDefaultValues(panel map[string]interface{}, originalProperties map[string]bool) {\n   558→\t// Get panel type for panel-specific defaults\n   559→\tpanelType := \"\"\n   560→\tif t, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n   561→\t\tpanelType = t\n   562→\t}\n   563→\n   564→\t// PanelModel defaults from frontend\n   565→\tdefaults := map[string]interface{}{\n   566→\t\t\"gridPos\": map[string]interface{}{\n   567→\t\t\t\"x\": 0, \"y\": 0, \"h\": 3, \"w\": 6,\n   568→\t\t},\n   569→\t\t\"targets\": []interface{}{\n   570→\t\t\tmap[string]interface{}{\"refId\": \"A\"},\n   571→\t\t},\n   572→\t\t\"cachedPluginOptions\": 576→\t\t\"fieldConfig\": map[string]interface{}{\n   577→\t\t\t\"defaults\":  map[string]interface{}{},\n   578→\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n   579→\t\t},\n   580→\t\t\"title\": \"\",\n   581→\t}\n   582→\n   583→\t// Add panel-specific defaults\n   584→\tif panelType == \"table\" {\n   585→\t\t// Remove legacy table properties (matches frontend getSaveModel filtering)\n   586→\t\t// Exception: preserve original properties for old table panels with autoMigrateFrom=\"table-old\"\n   587→\t\tlegacyTableProps := []string{\"pageSize\", \"scroll\", \"fontSize\", \"showHeader\", \"sort\"}\n   588→\t\tfor _, prop := range legacyTableProps {\n   589→\t\t\tif _, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n   590→\t\t\t\tif autoMigrateFrom, hasAutoMigrate := panel[\"autoMigrateFrom\"]; hasAutoMigrate && autoMigrateFrom == \"table-old\" {\n   591→\t\t\t\t\tif !originalProperties[prop] {\n   592→\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   593→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   594→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   595→\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   596→\t\t\t\t}\n   597→\t\t\t}\n   598→\t\t}\n   599→\t}\n   600→\n   601→\t// Remove properties that match defaults, but preserve properties that were originally present\n   602→\tfor prop, defaultValue := range defaults {\n   603→\t\tif panelValue, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n   604→\t\t\tif isEqual(panelValue, defaultValue) {\n   605→\t\t\t\t// Special case: fieldConfig - handle preservation of original custom object first\n   606→\t\t\t\tif prop == \"fieldConfig\" {\n   607→\t\t\t\t\t// Check if we need to preserve the custom object before removing fieldConfig\n   608→\t\t\t\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n   609→\t\t\t\t\t\t// Ensure fieldConfig structure exists with custom object\n   610→\t\t\t\t\t\tif fieldConfig, ok := panelValue.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   611→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif defaults, ok := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   612→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif _, hasCustom := defaults[\"custom\"]; !hasCustom {\n   613→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefaults[\"custom\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n   614→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   615→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t// Don't remove fieldConfig if we added custom back\n   616→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   617→\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   618→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   619→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   620→\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   621→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   622→\t\t\t\t\t// Only remove if it wasn't originally present in the input\n   623→\t\t\t\t\tif !originalProperties[prop] {\n   624→\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n   625→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   626→\t\t\t\t}\n   627→\t\t\t}\n   628→\t\t}\n   629→\t}\n   630→\n   631→\t// Remove empty targets arrays (frontend removes them in cleanup)\n   632→\tremoveIfDefaultValue(panel, \"targets\", []interface{}{})\n   633→\n   634→\t// Handle case where fieldConfig was removed but originally had custom object\n   635→\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n   636→\t\tif _, hasFieldConfig := panel[\"fieldConfig\"]; !hasFieldConfig {\n   637→\t\t\t// Recreate fieldConfig with custom object\n   638→\t\t\tpanel[\"fieldConfig\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n   639→\t\t\t\t\"defaults\": map[string]interface{}{\n   640→\t\t\t\t\t\"custom\": map[string]interface{}{},\n   641→\t\t\t\t},\n   642→\t\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n   643→\t\t\t}\n   644→\t\t}\n   645→\t}\n   646→\n   647→\t// Clean up fieldConfig to match frontend behavior\n   648→\tif fieldConfig, exists := panel[\"fieldConfig\"].(map[string]interface{}); exists {\n   649→\t\t// Clean up fieldConfig defaults to match frontend behavior\n   650→\t\tif defaults, hasDefaults := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); hasDefaults {\n   651→\t\t\t// Remove properties that frontend considers as defaults and omits\n   652→\t\t\tcleanupFieldConfigDefaults(defaults, panel)\n   653→\n   654→\t\t\t// Preserve custom object if it was originally present, even if empty\n   655→\t\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n   656→\t\t\t\tif _, hasCustom := defaults[\"custom\"]; !hasCustom {\n   657→\t\t\t\t\tdefaults[\"custom\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n   658→\t\t\t\t}\n   659→\t\t\t}\n   660→\t\t}\n   661→\t}\n   662→}\n   663→\n   664→// isEqual checks if two values are equal (simplified version)\n   665→func isEqual(a, b interface{}) bool {\n   666→\tif a == nil && b == nil {\n   667→\t\treturn true\n   668→\t}\n   669→\tif a == nil || b == nil {\n   670→\t\treturn false\n   671→\t}\n   672→\n   673→\t// For simple types, use direct comparison\n   674→\tswitch aVal := a.(type) {\n   675→\tcase bool:\n   676→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(bool); ok {\n   677→\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n   678→\t\t}\n   679→\tcase string:\n   680→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(string); ok {\n   681→\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n   682→\t\t}\n   683→\tcase float64:\n   684→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(float64); ok {\n   685→\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n   686→\t\t}\n   687→\tcase []interface{}:\n   688→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.([]interface{}); ok {\n   689→\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n   690→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   691→\t\t\t}\n   692→\t\t\tfor i, v := range aVal {\n   693→\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[i]) {\n   694→\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n   695→\t\t\t\t}\n   696→\t\t\t}\n   697→\t\t\treturn true\n   698→\t\t}\n   699→\tcase map[string]interface{}:\n   700→\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   701→\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n   702→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   703→\t\t\t}\n   704→\t\t\tfor k, v := range aVal {\n   705→\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[k]) {\n   706→\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n   707→\t\t\t\t}\n   708→\t\t\t}\n   709→\t\t\treturn true\n   710→\t\t}\n   711→\t}\n   712→\n   713→\treturn false\n   714→}\n   715→\n   716→// cleanupDashboardForSave applies the same cleanup logic as the frontend\n   717→func cleanupDashboardForSave(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   718→\tremoveNonPersistedProperties(dashboard)\n   719→\tremoveNullValues(dashboard)\n   720→\tcleanupTemplating(dashboard)\n   721→\tcleanupPanels(dashboard)\n   722→\tcleanupDashboardDefaults(dashboard)\n   723→}\n   724→\n   725→// removeNonPersistedProperties removes non-persisted dashboard properties\n   726→func removeNonPersistedProperties(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   727→\tnonPersistedProperties := map[string]bool{\n   728→\t\t\"events\":                           true,\n   729→\t\t\"meta\":                             true,\n   730→\t\t\"panels\":                           true, // handled specially below\n   731→\t\t\"templating\":                       true, // handled specially below\n   732→\t\t\"originalTime\":                     true,\n   733→\t\t\"originalTemplating\":               true,\n   734→\t\t\"originalLibraryPanels\":            true,\n   735→\t\t\"panelInEdit\":                      true,\n   736→\t\t\"panelInView\":                      true,\n   737→\t\t\"getVariablesFromState\":            true,\n   738→\t\t\"formatDate\":                       true,\n   739→\t\t\"appEventsSubscription\":            true,\n   740→\t\t\"panelsAffectedByVariableChange\":   true,\n   741→\t\t\"lastRefresh\":                      true,\n   742→\t\t\"timeRangeUpdatedDuringEditOrView\": true,\n   743→\t\t\"originalDashboard\":                true,\n   744→\t}\n   745→\n   746→\tfor k, v := range nonPersistedProperties {\n   747→\t\t// Do 760→// removeNullValues removes null values to match frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior\n   761→func removeNullValues(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   762→\t// This handles gnetId: null   775→func cleanupTemplatingVariables(templating map[string]interface{}) {\n   776→\tif list, ok := templating[\"list\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n   777→\t\tfor _, variableInterface := range list {\n cleanupVariable cleans up individual variable properties\n   786→func cleanupVariable(variable map[string]interface{}) {\n   787→\t// Remove null datasource\n   788→\tremoveIfDefaultValue(variable, \"datasource\", nil)\n   789→\n   790→\t// Remove properties that frontend omits in getSaveModel\n   791→\tdelete(variable, \"index\")\n   792→\n   793→\t// Apply variable type-specific logic\n   794→\tif variableType, ok := variable[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n   795→\t\tswitch variableType {\n   796→\t\tcase \"query\":\n   797→\t\t\t// Query variables: keep options: [] if refresh !== never (matches frontend getSaveModel logic)\n   798→\t\t\trefresh := schemaversion.GetIntValue(variable, \"refresh\", 1) // Default to 1 (onDashboardLoad) if not specified\n   799→\t\t\tif refresh != 0 {                                            // 0 = VariableRefreshNever\n   800→\t\t\t\tif _, hasOptions := variable[\"options\"]; !hasOptions {\n   801→\t\t\t\t\tvariable[\"options\"] = []interface{}{}\n   802→\t\t\t\t}\n   803→\t\t\t}\n   804→\t\tcase \"constant\":\n   805→\t\t\t// Constant variables: remove options completely\n   806→\t\t\tdelete(variable, \"options\")\n   807→\t\tcase \"datasource\":\n   808→\t\t\t// Datasource variables: always set options to empty array\n   809→\t\t\tvariable[\"options\"] = []interface{}{}\n   810→\t\tcase \"custom\":\n   811→\t\t\t// Custom variables: no special handling (just return rest)\n   812→\t\t\t// This is the default behavior - no additional processing needed\n   813→\t\tcase \"textbox\":\n   814→\t\t\t// Textbox variables: handle query vs originalQuery logic\n   815→\t\t\t// For now, just return rest (no special handling needed for basic cases)\n   816→\t\tcase \"adhoc\":\n   817→\t\t\t// Adhoc variables: no special handling\n   818→\t\t\t// This is the default behavior - no additional processing needed\n   819→\t\t}\n   820→\t}\n   821→}\n   822→\n   823→// cleanupPanels cleans up panels and ensures panels property always exists\n   824→func cleanupPanels(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n   825→\tif panels, ok := dashboard[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n   826→\t\t// Filter out repeated panels (matches frontend getPanelSaveModels behavior)\n   827→\t\t// Frontend filters: !(panel.repeatPanelId || panel.repeatedByRow)\n   828→\t\tfilteredPanels := []interface{}{}\n   829→\t\tfor _, panelInterface := range panels {\n   830→\t\t\tif panel, ok := panelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   831→\t\t\t\t// Skip panels with repeatPanelId or repeatedByRow\n   832→\t\t\t\tif _, 843→\t\tsortPanelsByGridPosition(filteredPanels)\n   844→\t\tdashboard[\"panels\"] = filteredPanels\n   845→\t} else {\n   846→\t\t// Ensure panels property exists even if empty (matches frontend behavior)\n   847→\t\tdashboard[\"panels\"] = []interface{}{}\n   848→\t}\n   849→}\n   850→\n   851→// cleanupPanelList cleans up all panels including nested ones\n   852→func cleanupPanelList(panels false)\n   856→\n   857→\t\t\t// Handle nested panels in row panels\n   858→\t\t\tif nestedPanels, ok := panel[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n   859→\t\t\t\tfor _, nestedPanelInterface := range 863→\t\t\t\t}\n   864→\t\t\t}\n   865→\t\t}\n   866→\t}\n   867→}\n   868→\n   869→// sortPanelsByGridPosition sorts panels by grid position (matches frontend sortPanelsByGridPos behavior)\n   870→func sortPanelsByGridPosition(panels []interface{}) {\n   871→\tsort.SliceStable(panels, func(i, j int) bool {\n   872→\t\tpanelA, okA := panels[i].(map[string]interface{})\n   873→\t\tpanelB, okB := panels[j].(map[string]interface{})\n   874→\t\tif !okA || !okB {\n   875→\t\t\treturn false\n   876→\t\t}\n   877→\n   878→\t\t// Get gridPos or use default values if missing\n   879→\t\tgridPosA, okA := panelA[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   880→\t\tgridPosB, okB := panelB[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n   881→\n   882→\t\t// Default gridPos values (matches frontend PanelModel defaults)\n   883→\t\tdefaultY := float64(0)\n   884→\t\tdefaultX := float64(0)\n   885→\n   886→\t\tyA := defaultY\n   887→\t\tif okA {\n   888→\t\t\tif y, ok := gridPosA[\"y\"].(float64); ok {\n   889→\t\t\t\tyA = y\n   890→\t\t\t} else if y, ok := gridPosA[\"y\"].(int); ok {\n   891→\t\t\t\tyA = float64(y)\n   892→\t\t\t}\n   893→\t\t}\n   894→\n   895→\t\tyB := defaultY\n   896→\t\tif okB {\n   897→\t\t\tif y, ok := gridPosB[\"y\"].(float64); ok {\n   898→\t\t\t\tyB = y\n   899→\t\t\t} else if y, ok := gridPosB[\"y\"].(int); ok {\n   900→\t\t\t\tyB = float64(y)\n   901→\t\t\t}\n   902→\t\t}\n   903→\n   904→\t\tif yA == yB {\n   905→\t\t\txA := defaultX\n   906→\t\t\tif okA {\n   907→\t\t\t\tif x, ok := gridPosA[\"x\"].(float64); ok {\n   908→\t\t\t\t\txA = x\n   909→\t\t\t\t} else if x, ok := gridPosA[\"x\"].(int); ok {\n   910→\t\t\t\t\txA = float64(x)\n   911→\t\t\t\t}\n   912→\t\t\t}\n   913→\n   914→\t\t\txB := defaultX\n   915→\t\t\tif okB {\n   916→\t\t\t\tif x, ok := gridPosB[\"x\"].(float64); ok {\n   917→\t\t\t\t\txB = x\n   918→\t\t\t\t} else if x, ok := gridPosB[\"x\"].(int); ok {\n   919→\t\t\t\t\txB = float64(x)\n   920→\t\t\t\t}\n   921→\t\t\t}\n   922→\t\t\treturn xA < xB\n   923→\t\t}\n   924→\t\treturn yA < yB\n   925→\t})\n   926→}\n   927→\n   928→// cleanupRowPanelProperties removes default row panel properties that frontend filters out\n   929→func cleanupRowPanelProperties(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n   930→\tpanelType, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string)\n   931→\tif !ok || panelType != \"row\" {\n   932→\t\treturn\n   933→\t}\n   934→\n   935→\t// Remove repeat if empty string (default value)\n   936→\tremoveIfDefaultValue(panel, \"repeat\", \"\")\n   937→}\n   938→\n   939→// applyPanelAutoMigration applies the same auto-migration logic as the frontend PanelModel constructor\n   940→func applyPanelAutoMigration(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n   941→\tpanelType, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string)\n   942→\tif !ok {\n   943→\t\treturn\n   944→\t}\n   945→\n   946→\tvar newType string\n   947→\n   948→\t// Graph needs special logic as it can be migrated to multiple panels\n   949→\t// Including graphite which was previously migrated to graph in the schema version 2 migration in DashboardMigrator.ts\n   950→\t// but this was a bug because in there graphite was set to graph, but since those migrations run\n   951→\t// after PanelModel.restoreModel where autoMigrateFrom is set, this caused the graph migration to be skipped.\n   952→\t// And this resulted in a dashboard with invalid panels.\n   953→\tif panelType == \"graph\" || panelType == \"graphite\" {\n   954→\t\t// Check xaxis mode for special cases\n   955→\t\tnewType = getGraphAutoMigration(panel)\n   956→\t} else {\n   957→\t\t// Check autoMigrateAngular mapping\n   958→\t\tautoMigrateAngular := map[string]string{\n   959→\t\t\t\"table-old\":                \"table\",\n   960→\t\t\t\"singlestat\":               \"stat\",\n   961→\t\t\t\"grafana-singlestat-panel\": \"stat\",\n   962→\t\t\t\"grafana-piechart-panel\":   \"piechart\",\n   963→\t\t\t\"grafana-worldmap-panel\":   \"geomap\",\n   964→\t\t\t\"natel-discrete-panel\":     \"state-timeline\",\n   965→\t\t}\n   966→\n   967→\t\tif mappedType, exists := \"\" {\n   974→\t\tpanel[\"autoMigrateFrom\"] = panelType\n   975→\t\tpanel[\"type\"] = newType\n   976→\t}\n   977→}\n   978→\n   979→func getGraphAutoMigration(panel map[string]interface{}) string {\n   980→\tnewType := \"\"\n   981→\tif xaxis, ok := panel[\"xaxis\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   982→\t\tif mode, ok := xaxis[\"mode\"].(string); ok {\n   983→\t\t\tswitch mode {\n   984→\t\t\tcase \"series\":\n   985→\t\t\t\t// Check legend values for bargauge\n   986→\t\t\t\tif legend, ok := panel[\"legend\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n   987→\t\t\t\t\tif values, ok := legend[\"values\"].(bool); ok && values {\n   988→\t\t\t\t\t\tnewType = \"bargauge\"\n   989→\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n   990→\t\t\t\t\t\tnewType = \"barchart\"\n   991→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   992→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   993→\t\t\t\t\tnewType = \"barchart\"\n   994→\t\t\t\t}\n   995→\t\t\tcase \"histogram\":\n   996→\t\t\t\tnewType = \"histogram\"\n   997→\t\t\t}\n   998→\t\t}\n   999→\t}\n  1000→\n  1001→\t// Default graph migration to timeseries\n  1002→\tif newType == \"\" {\n  1003→\t\tnewType = \"timeseries\"\n  1004→\t}\n  1005→\n  1006→\treturn newType\n  1007→}\n  1008→\n  1009→// removeNullValuesRecursively removes null values from nested objects and arrays\n  1010→// This matches the frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior\n  1011→func removeNullValuesRecursively(data interface{}) {\n  1012→\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(data, \"\")\n  1013→}\n  1014→\n  1015→// removeNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext removes null values from nested objects and arrays\n  1016→// This matches the frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior in getSaveModelClone()\n  1017→func removeNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(data interface{}, panelType string) {\n  1018→\tswitch v := data.(type) {\n  1019→\tcase map[string]interface{}:\n  1020→\t\t// Remove null values from map\n  1021→\t\tfor key, value := range v {\n  1022→\t\t\tif value == nil {\n  1023→\t\t\t\t// Frontend Recursively process nested values\n  1028→\t\t\t\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(value, panelType)\n  1029→\t\t\t}\n  1030→\t\t}\n  1031→\tcase []interface{}:\n  1032→\t\t// Process array elements\n  1033→\t\tfor _, item := range v {\n  1034→\t\t\tif item != nil {\n  1035→\t\t\t\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(item, panelType)\n  1036→\t\t\t}\n  1037→\t\t}\n  1038→\t}\n  1039→}\n  1040→\n  1041→// removeIfDefaultValue removes the key from the map if its value equals the defaultValue\n  1042→func removeIfDefaultValue(data map[string]interface{}, key string, defaultValue interface{}) {\n  1043→\tif val, ok := data[key]; ok && isEqual(val, defaultValue) {\n  1044→\t\tdelete(data, key)\n  1045→\t}\n  1046→}\n  1047→\n  1048→// cleanupDashboardDefaults \"hideControls\", false)\n  1055→\n  1056→\t// Remove dashboard id if it's null\n  1057→\tremoveIfDefaultValue(dashboard, \"id\", nil)\n  1058→\n  1059→\t// Remove version property - it's managed by the backend metadata, not the spec\n  1060→\tdelete(dashboard, \"version\")\n  1061→\n  1062→\t// Remove transient properties that frontend filters out during getSaveModelClone()\n  1063→\t// These cleanupFieldConfigDefaults removes properties that frontend considers as defaults and omits\n  1070→func cleanupFieldConfigDefaults(defaults map[string]interface{}, panel map[string]interface{}) {\n  1071→\t// Don't remove mappings, color objects, or unit properties - frontend preserves them\n  1072→\n  1073→\t// Remove empty custom objects from migrated singlestat panels (frontend filters them out)\n  1074→\tif custom, exists := defaults[\"custom\"].(map[string]interface{}); exists {\n  1075→\t\tif len(custom) == 0 {\n  1076→\t\t\t// Check if this is a migrated singlestat panel by looking 1090→\t\t\t\t\tif _, hasFixedColor := color[\"fixedColor\"].(string); hasFixedColor {\n  1091→\t\t\t\t\t\tif mode, hasMode := color[\"mode\"].(string); hasMode && mode == \"fixed\" {\n trackOriginalTransformations marks panels that had transformations in the original input\n  1110→// This is needed to match frontend hasOwnProperty behavior\n  1111→func 1121→// trackPanelOriginalTransformations recursively tracks transformations in panels and nested panels\n  1122→func trackPanelOriginalTransformations(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n  1123→\t// map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"defaults\":  map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n\t\t},\n\t\t\"title\": \"\",\n\t}\n\n\t// Add panel-specific defaults\n\tif panelType == \"table\" {\n\t\t// Remove legacy table properties (matches frontend getSaveModel filtering)\n\t\t// Exception: preserve original properties for old table panels with autoMigrateFrom=\"table-old\"\n\t\tlegacyTableProps := []string{\"pageSize\", \"scroll\", \"fontSize\", \"showHeader\", \"sort\"}\n\t\tfor _, prop := range legacyTableProps {\n\t\t\tif _, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n\t\t\t\tif autoMigrateFrom, hasAutoMigrate := panel[\"autoMigrateFrom\"]; hasAutoMigrate && autoMigrateFrom == \"table-old\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tif !originalProperties[prop] {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Remove properties that match defaults, but preserve properties that were originally present\n\tfor prop, defaultValue := range defaults {\n\t\tif panelValue, exists := panel[prop]; exists {\n\t\t\tif isEqual(panelValue, defaultValue) {\n\t\t\t\t// Special case: fieldConfig - handle preservation of original custom object first\n\t\t\t\tif prop == \"fieldConfig\" {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Check if we need to preserve the custom object before removing fieldConfig\n\t\t\t\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// Ensure fieldConfig structure exists with custom object\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif fieldConfig, ok := panelValue.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif defaults, ok := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif _, hasCustom := defaults[\"custom\"]; !hasCustom {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefaults[\"custom\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t// Don't remove fieldConfig if we added custom back\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Only remove if it wasn't originally present in the input\n\t\t\t\t\tif !originalProperties[prop] {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tdelete(panel, prop)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Remove empty targets arrays (frontend removes them in cleanup)\n\tremoveIfDefaultValue(panel, \"targets\", []interface{}{})\n\n\t// Handle case where fieldConfig was removed but originally had custom object\n\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n\t\tif _, hasFieldConfig := panel[\"fieldConfig\"]; !hasFieldConfig {\n\t\t\t// Recreate fieldConfig with custom object\n\t\t\tpanel[\"fieldConfig\"] = map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"defaults\": map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\t\"custom\": map[string]interface{}{},\n\t\t\t\t},\n\t\t\t\t\"overrides\": []interface{}{},\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Clean up fieldConfig to match frontend behavior\n\tif fieldConfig, exists := panel[\"fieldConfig\"].(map[string]interface{}); exists {\n\t\t// Clean up fieldConfig defaults to match frontend behavior\n\t\tif defaults, hasDefaults := fieldConfig[\"defaults\"].(map[string]interface{}); hasDefaults {\n\t\t\t// Remove properties that frontend considers as defaults and omits\n\t\t\tcleanupFieldConfigDefaults(defaults, panel)\n\n\t\t\t// Preserve custom object if it was originally present, even if empty\n\t\t\tif panel[\"_originallyHadFieldConfigCustom\"] == true {\n\t\t\t\tif _, hasCustom := defaults[\"custom\"]; !hasCustom {\n\t\t\t\t\tdefaults[\"custom\"] = map[string]interface{}{}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// isEqual checks if two values are equal (simplified version)\nfunc isEqual(a, b interface{}) bool {\n\tif a == nil && b == nil {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\tif a == nil || b == nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// For simple types, use direct comparison\n\tswitch aVal := a.(type) {\n\tcase bool:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(bool); ok {\n\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n\t\t}\n\tcase string:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(string); ok {\n\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n\t\t}\n\tcase float64:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(float64); ok {\n\t\t\treturn aVal == bVal\n\t\t}\n\tcase []interface{}:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor i, v := range aVal {\n\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[i]) {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\tcase map[string]interface{}:\n\t\tif bVal, ok := b.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\tif len(aVal) != len(bVal) {\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor k, v := range aVal {\n\t\t\t\tif !isEqual(v, bVal[k]) {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// cleanupDashboardForSave applies the same cleanup logic as the frontend\nfunc cleanupDashboardForSave(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tremoveNonPersistedProperties(dashboard)\n\tremoveNullValues(dashboard)\n\tcleanupTemplating(dashboard)\n\tcleanupPanels(dashboard)\n\tcleanupDashboardDefaults(dashboard)\n}\n\n// removeNonPersistedProperties removes non-persisted dashboard properties\nfunc removeNonPersistedProperties(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tnonPersistedProperties := map[string]bool{\n\t\t\"events\":                           true,\n\t\t\"meta\":                             true,\n\t\t\"panels\":                           true, // handled specially below\n\t\t\"templating\":                       true, // handled specially below\n\t\t\"originalTime\":                     true,\n\t\t\"originalTemplating\":               true,\n\t\t\"originalLibraryPanels\":            true,\n\t\t\"panelInEdit\":                      true,\n\t\t\"panelInView\":                      true,\n\t\t\"getVariablesFromState\":            true,\n\t\t\"formatDate\":                       true,\n\t\t\"appEventsSubscription\":            true,\n\t\t\"panelsAffectedByVariableChange\":   true,\n\t\t\"lastRefresh\":                      true,\n\t\t\"timeRangeUpdatedDuringEditOrView\": true,\n\t\t\"originalDashboard\":                true,\n\t}\n\n\tfor k, v := range nonPersistedProperties {\n\t\t// Do not remove \"panels\" and \"templating\" here, as they are handled specially\n\t\tif (k == \"panels\" || k == \"templating\") && v {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tif v {\n\t\t\tdelete(dashboard, k)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Remove properties that frontend omits in getSaveModel\n\tdelete(dashboard, \"variables\")\n}\n\n// removeNullValues removes null values to match frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior\nfunc removeNullValues(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\t// This handles gnetId: null and other null properties\n\tremoveIfDefaultValue(dashboard, \"gnetId\", nil)\n}\n\n// cleanupTemplating cleans up templating to match frontend's getTemplatingSaveModel behavior\nfunc cleanupTemplating(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tif templating, ok := dashboard[\"templating\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\tremoveNullValuesRecursively(templating)\n\t\tcleanupTemplatingVariables(templating)\n\t}\n}\n\n// cleanupTemplatingVariables applies variable adapter logic\nfunc cleanupTemplatingVariables(templating map[string]interface{}) {\n\tif list, ok := templating[\"list\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\tfor _, variableInterface := range list {\n\t\t\tif variable, ok := variableInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\tcleanupVariable(variable)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// cleanupVariable cleans up individual variable properties\nfunc cleanupVariable(variable map[string]interface{}) {\n\t// Remove null datasource\n\tremoveIfDefaultValue(variable, \"datasource\", nil)\n\n\t// Remove properties that frontend omits in getSaveModel\n\tdelete(variable, \"index\")\n\n\t// Apply variable type-specific logic\n\tif variableType, ok := variable[\"type\"].(string); ok {\n\t\tswitch variableType {\n\t\tcase \"query\":\n\t\t\t// Query variables: keep options: [] if refresh !== never (matches frontend getSaveModel logic)\n\t\t\trefresh := schemaversion.GetIntValue(variable, \"refresh\", 1) // Default to 1 (onDashboardLoad) if not specified\n\t\t\tif refresh != 0 {                                            // 0 = VariableRefreshNever\n\t\t\t\tif _, hasOptions := variable[\"options\"]; !hasOptions {\n\t\t\t\t\tvariable[\"options\"] = []interface{}{}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase \"constant\":\n\t\t\t// Constant variables: remove options completely\n\t\t\tdelete(variable, \"options\")\n\t\tcase \"datasource\":\n\t\t\t// Datasource variables: always set options to empty array\n\t\t\tvariable[\"options\"] = []interface{}{}\n\t\tcase \"custom\":\n\t\t\t// Custom variables: no special handling (just return rest)\n\t\t\t// This is the default behavior - no additional processing needed\n\t\tcase \"textbox\":\n\t\t\t// Textbox variables: handle query vs originalQuery logic\n\t\t\t// For now, just return rest (no special handling needed for basic cases)\n\t\tcase \"adhoc\":\n\t\t\t// Adhoc variables: no special handling\n\t\t\t// This is the default behavior - no additional processing needed\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// cleanupPanels cleans up panels and ensures panels property always exists\nfunc cleanupPanels(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tif panels, ok := dashboard[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t// Filter out repeated panels (matches frontend getPanelSaveModels behavior)\n\t\t// Frontend filters: !(panel.repeatPanelId || panel.repeatedByRow)\n\t\tfilteredPanels := []interface{}{}\n\t\tfor _, panelInterface := range panels {\n\t\t\tif panel, ok := panelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t// Skip panels with repeatPanelId or repeatedByRow\n\t\t\t\tif _, hasRepeatPanelId := panel[\"repeatPanelId\"]; hasRepeatPanelId {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif _, hasRepeatedByRow := panel[\"repeatedByRow\"]; hasRepeatedByRow {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tfilteredPanels = append(filteredPanels, panel)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tcleanupPanelList(filteredPanels)\n\t\tsortPanelsByGridPosition(filteredPanels)\n\t\tdashboard[\"panels\"] = filteredPanels\n\t} else {\n\t\t// Ensure panels property exists even if empty (matches frontend behavior)\n\t\tdashboard[\"panels\"] = []interface{}{}\n\t}\n}\n\n// cleanupPanelList cleans up all panels including nested ones\nfunc cleanupPanelList(panels []interface{}) {\n\tfor _, panelInterface := range panels {\n\t\tif panel, ok := panelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\tcleanupPanelForSaveWithContext(panel, false)\n\n\t\t\t// Handle nested panels in row panels\n\t\t\tif nestedPanels, ok := panel[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\tfor _, nestedPanelInterface := range nestedPanels {\n\t\t\t\t\tif nestedPanel, ok := nestedPanelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcleanupPanelForSaveWithContext(nestedPanel, true)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// sortPanelsByGridPosition sorts panels by grid position (matches frontend sortPanelsByGridPos behavior)\nfunc sortPanelsByGridPosition(panels []interface{}) {\n\tsort.SliceStable(panels, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\tpanelA, okA := panels[i].(map[string]interface{})\n\t\tpanelB, okB := panels[j].(map[string]interface{})\n\t\tif !okA || !okB {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Get gridPos or use default values if missing\n\t\tgridPosA, okA := panelA[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n\t\tgridPosB, okB := panelB[\"gridPos\"].(map[string]interface{})\n\n\t\t// Default gridPos values (matches frontend PanelModel defaults)\n\t\tdefaultY := float64(0)\n\t\tdefaultX := float64(0)\n\n\t\tyA := defaultY\n\t\tif okA {\n\t\t\tif y, ok := gridPosA[\"y\"].(float64); ok {\n\t\t\t\tyA = y\n\t\t\t} else if y, ok := gridPosA[\"y\"].(int); ok {\n\t\t\t\tyA = float64(y)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tyB := defaultY\n\t\tif okB {\n\t\t\tif y, ok := gridPosB[\"y\"].(float64); ok {\n\t\t\t\tyB = y\n\t\t\t} else if y, ok := gridPosB[\"y\"].(int); ok {\n\t\t\t\tyB = float64(y)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif yA == yB {\n\t\t\txA := defaultX\n\t\t\tif okA {\n\t\t\t\tif x, ok := gridPosA[\"x\"].(float64); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\txA = x\n\t\t\t\t} else if x, ok := gridPosA[\"x\"].(int); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\txA = float64(x)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\txB := defaultX\n\t\t\tif okB {\n\t\t\t\tif x, ok := gridPosB[\"x\"].(float64); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\txB = x\n\t\t\t\t} else if x, ok := gridPosB[\"x\"].(int); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\txB = float64(x)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn xA < xB\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn yA < yB\n\t})\n}\n\n// cleanupRowPanelProperties removes default row panel properties that frontend filters out\nfunc cleanupRowPanelProperties(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n\tpanelType, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string)\n\tif !ok || panelType != \"row\" {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Remove repeat if empty string (default value)\n\tremoveIfDefaultValue(panel, \"repeat\", \"\")\n}\n\n// applyPanelAutoMigration applies the same auto-migration logic as the frontend PanelModel constructor\nfunc applyPanelAutoMigration(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n\tpanelType, ok := panel[\"type\"].(string)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tvar newType string\n\n\t// Graph needs special logic as it can be migrated to multiple panels\n\t// Including graphite which was previously migrated to graph in the schema version 2 migration in DashboardMigrator.ts\n\t// but this was a bug because in there graphite was set to graph, but since those migrations run\n\t// after PanelModel.restoreModel where autoMigrateFrom is set, this caused the graph migration to be skipped.\n\t// And this resulted in a dashboard with invalid panels.\n\tif panelType == \"graph\" || panelType == \"graphite\" {\n\t\t// Check xaxis mode for special cases\n\t\tnewType = getGraphAutoMigration(panel)\n\t} else {\n\t\t// Check autoMigrateAngular mapping\n\t\tautoMigrateAngular := map[string]string{\n\t\t\t\"table-old\":                \"table\",\n\t\t\t\"singlestat\":               \"stat\",\n\t\t\t\"grafana-singlestat-panel\": \"stat\",\n\t\t\t\"grafana-piechart-panel\":   \"piechart\",\n\t\t\t\"grafana-worldmap-panel\":   \"geomap\",\n\t\t\t\"natel-discrete-panel\":     \"state-timeline\",\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif mappedType, exists := autoMigrateAngular[panelType]; exists {\n\t\t\tnewType = mappedType\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Apply auto-migration if a new type was determined\n\tif newType != \"\" {\n\t\tpanel[\"autoMigrateFrom\"] = panelType\n\t\tpanel[\"type\"] = newType\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc getGraphAutoMigration(panel map[string]interface{}) string {\n\tnewType := \"\"\n\tif xaxis, ok := panel[\"xaxis\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\tif mode, ok := xaxis[\"mode\"].(string); ok {\n\t\t\tswitch mode {\n\t\t\tcase \"series\":\n\t\t\t\t// Check legend values for bargauge\n\t\t\t\tif legend, ok := panel[\"legend\"].(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tif values, ok := legend[\"values\"].(bool); ok && values {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tnewType = \"bargauge\"\n\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tnewType = \"barchart\"\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tnewType = \"barchart\"\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase \"histogram\":\n\t\t\t\tnewType = \"histogram\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Default graph migration to timeseries\n\tif newType == \"\" {\n\t\tnewType = \"timeseries\"\n\t}\n\n\treturn newType\n}\n\n// removeNullValuesRecursively removes null values from nested objects and arrays\n// This matches the frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior\nfunc removeNullValuesRecursively(data interface{}) {\n\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(data, \"\")\n}\n\n// removeNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext removes null values from nested objects and arrays\n// This matches the frontend's JSON.stringify/parse behavior in getSaveModelClone()\nfunc removeNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(data interface{}, panelType string) {\n\tswitch v := data.(type) {\n\tcase map[string]interface{}:\n\t\t// Remove null values from map\n\t\tfor key, value := range v {\n\t\t\tif value == nil {\n\t\t\t\t// Frontend removes null values via JSON serialization, so we should too\n\t\t\t\t// No special case needed for threshold steps\n\t\t\t\tdelete(v, key)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Recursively process nested values\n\t\t\t\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(value, panelType)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase []interface{}:\n\t\t// Process array elements\n\t\tfor _, item := range v {\n\t\t\tif item != nil {\n\t\t\t\tremoveNullValuesRecursivelyWithContext(item, panelType)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// removeIfDefaultValue removes the key from the map if its value equals the defaultValue\nfunc removeIfDefaultValue(data map[string]interface{}, key string, defaultValue interface{}) {\n\tif val, ok := data[key]; ok && isEqual(val, defaultValue) {\n\t\tdelete(data, key)\n\t}\n}\n\n// cleanupDashboardDefaults removes dashboard-level default values that frontend filters out\nfunc cleanupDashboardDefaults(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\t// Remove style if it's the default \"dark\" value\n\tremoveIfDefaultValue(dashboard, \"style\", \"dark\")\n\n\t// Remove hideControls if it's the default false value\n\tremoveIfDefaultValue(dashboard, \"hideControls\", false)\n\n\t// Remove dashboard id if it's null\n\tremoveIfDefaultValue(dashboard, \"id\", nil)\n\n\t// Remove version property - it's managed by the backend metadata, not the spec\n\tdelete(dashboard, \"version\")\n\n\t// Remove transient properties that frontend filters out during getSaveModelClone()\n\t// These properties are lost during frontend's property copying loop in getSaveModelCloneOld()\n\tdelete(dashboard, \"iteration\") // Template variable iteration timestamp\n\tdelete(dashboard, \"nav\")       // Removed after V7 migration\n\tdelete(dashboard, \"pulldowns\") // Removed after V6 migration - frontend doesn't have this property\n}\n\n// cleanupFieldConfigDefaults removes properties that frontend considers as defaults and omits\nfunc cleanupFieldConfigDefaults(defaults map[string]interface{}, panel map[string]interface{}) {\n\t// Don't remove mappings, color objects, or unit properties - frontend preserves them\n\n\t// Remove empty custom objects from migrated singlestat panels (frontend filters them out)\n\tif custom, exists := defaults[\"custom\"].(map[string]interface{}); exists {\n\t\tif len(custom) == 0 {\n\t\t\t// Check if this is a migrated singlestat panel by looking for characteristic properties\n\t\t\tisMigratedSinglestat := false\n\n\t\t\t// Check for autoMigrateFrom property first\n\t\t\tif autoMigrateFrom, exists := panel[\"autoMigrateFrom\"]; exists {\n\t\t\t\tif autoMigrateFrom == \"singlestat\" || autoMigrateFrom == \"grafana-singlestat-panel\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tisMigratedSinglestat = true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// If autoMigrateFrom is not present, check for characteristic migrated singlestat properties\n\t\t\tif !isMigratedSinglestat {\n\t\t\t\t// Check for color with fixedColor and mode \"fixed\" (from sparkline migration)\n\t\t\t\tif color, hasColor := defaults[\"color\"].(map[string]interface{}); hasColor {\n\t\t\t\t\tif _, hasFixedColor := color[\"fixedColor\"].(string); hasFixedColor {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif mode, hasMode := color[\"mode\"].(string); hasMode && mode == \"fixed\" {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t// Check for mappings array (from valueMaps migration)\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif _, hasMappings := defaults[\"mappings\"].([]interface{}); hasMappings {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tisMigratedSinglestat = true\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Only remove empty custom objects for migrated singlestat panels\n\t\t\tif isMigratedSinglestat {\n\t\t\t\tdelete(defaults, \"custom\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// trackOriginalTransformations marks panels that had transformations in the original input\n// This is needed to match frontend hasOwnProperty behavior\nfunc trackOriginalTransformations(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tif panels, ok := dashboard[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\tfor _, panelInterface := range panels {\n\t\t\tif panel, ok := panelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\ttrackPanelOriginalTransformations(panel)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// trackPanelOriginalTransformations recursively tracks transformations in panels and nested panels\nfunc trackPanelOriginalTransformations(panel map[string]interface{}) {\n\t// Mark if this panel had transformations in original input\n\tif _, hasTransformations := panel[\"transformations\"]; hasTransformations {\n\t\tpanel[\"_originallyHadTransformations\"] = true\n\t}\n\n\t// Handle nested panels in row panels\n\tif nestedPanels, ok := panel[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\tfor _, nestedPanelInterface := range nestedPanels {\n\t\t\tif nestedPanel, ok := nestedPanelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\ttrackPanelOriginalTransformations(nestedPanel)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// trackOriginalFieldConfigCustom marks panels that had fieldConfig.defaults.custom in the original input\n// This is needed to match frontend hasOwnProperty behavior and preserve empty custom objects\nfunc trackOriginalFieldConfigCustom(dashboard map[string]interface{}) {\n\tif panels, ok := dashboard[\"panels\"].([]interface{}); ok {\n\t\tfor _, panelInterface := range panels {\n\t\t\tif panel, ok := panelInterface.(map[string]interface{}); ok {\n\t\t\t\ttrackPanelOriginalFieldConfigCustom(panel)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// trackPanelOriginalFieldConfigCustom recursively tracks fieldConfig.defaults.custom in panels and nested panels\nfunc
